##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 1
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, that is designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, technical specifications, product designs, software code, marketing plans, customer lists, supplier agreements, research and development projects, and any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known to the public.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all derivatives, summaries, compilations, or analyses of such information, regardless of who prepares them. Information will not be considered Confidential Information if it: (a) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure by the Disclosing Party; (b) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party; (c) is lawfully obtained by the Receiving Party from a third party without restriction; or (d) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reference to or use of the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that the Disclosing Party retains all rights, title, and interest in its Confidential Information and that no license or other rights are granted by implication or otherwise under any intellectual property rights. The Receiving Party agrees to use the Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or engaging in a potential business relationship with the Disclosing Party (the "Permitted Purpose") and for no other purpose without prior written consent.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Permitted Purpose**: The Receiving Party may use Confidential Information only for the Permitted Purpose and must not exploit it for competitive advantage or unauthorized commercial gain.  

2. **Disclosure Limitations**: Confidential Information may only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or advisors who have a legitimate need to know and who are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

3. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying structure or design.  

4. **No Copying or Reproduction**: The Receiving Party shall not copy, reproduce, or duplicate Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the Permitted Purpose.  

5. **Security Measures**: The Receiving Party must implement reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

6. **No Publicity**: The Receiving Party shall not issue press releases, public announcements, or marketing materials referencing the Disclosing Party or the Confidential Information without prior written consent.  

7. **No Transfer of Rights**: The Receiving Party shall not assign, transfer, or sell any rights to Confidential Information without the Disclosing Party’s express written permission.  

8. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws, regulations, and industry standards in handling Confidential Information, including data protection laws.  

9. **No Circumvention**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to circumvent the Disclosing Party’s business relationships or contractual obligations.  

10. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party must immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information.  

11. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

12. **No Modification**: The Receiving Party shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works from Confidential Information without the Disclosing Party’s prior written approval.  

13. **No Use in Litigation**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information in any legal proceeding or dispute without a court order or the Disclosing Party’s consent.  

14. **Third-Party Confidentiality**: The Receiving Party shall ensure that any third parties with access to Confidential Information adhere to the same restrictions as outlined in this Agreement.  

15. **No Implied Licenses**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any implied licenses or rights to the Disclosing Party’s intellectual property beyond the Permitted Purpose.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"), unless terminated earlier as provided herein. The Term may be renewed by mutual written agreement of the parties for additional periods of equal or shorter duration. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing thirty (30) days’ prior written notice to the other party. Upon termination, the Receiving Party’s obligations under this Agreement shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] with respect to Confidential Information that constitutes trade secrets and for [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] for all other Confidential Information. The Disclosing Party may also terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Receiving Party breaches any material term of this Agreement and fails to cure such breach within [insert cure period, e.g., fifteen (15) days] of receiving notice. All provisions of this Agreement that by their nature should survive termination (e.g., confidentiality obligations, remedies, and dispute resolution) shall remain in effect.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure or use of Confidential Information may cause irreparable harm to the Disclosing Party, for which monetary damages may be inadequate. Accordingly, the Disclosing Party shall be entitled to seek injunctive or other equitable relief to prevent or restrain such breach, in addition to any other remedies available at law or in equity. The Receiving Party shall be liable for all direct, indirect, consequential, and punitive damages arising from its breach of this Agreement, including but not limited to lost profits, reputational harm, and costs of enforcement. The Disclosing Party may also recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in enforcing this Agreement. The remedies set forth herein are cumulative and not exclusive of any other remedies available under applicable law.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert governing law jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising out of or relating to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration provider, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert venue, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the state and federal courts located in [insert venue, e.g., the County of San Francisco] for such purposes.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 2
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, any non-public, sensitive, or proprietary data, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means, that is designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

Confidential Information encompasses: (a) trade secrets, business strategies, financial records, marketing plans, and operational procedures; (b) technical data, inventions, software, algorithms, and research; (c) customer lists, supplier details, and contractual terms; (d) any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known to the public; and (e) any derivatives, analyses, or compilations of the foregoing.  

The scope of Confidential Information excludes information that: (i) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient; (ii) was lawfully known to the Recipient prior to disclosure by the Discloser; (iii) is independently developed by the Recipient without reliance on the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (iv) is rightfully obtained by the Recipient from a third party without breach of confidentiality obligations.  

The Recipient acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information could cause irreparable harm to the Discloser. Accordingly, the Recipient agrees to exercise the same degree of care to protect such information as it would with its own confidential material, but no less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as expressly authorized in writing by the Discloser.  

2. **Limited Disclosure**: The Recipient may disclose Confidential Information only to its employees, contractors, or advisors who have a need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as stringent as those herein.  

3. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information provided in tangible or electronic form.  

4. **No Copying**: The Recipient shall not copy, reproduce, or duplicate Confidential Information except as necessary for the authorized purpose and with the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

5. **No Publicity**: The Recipient shall not issue press releases, marketing materials, or other public statements referencing the Discloser or the Confidential Information without express written approval.  

6. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement and maintain reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

7. **No Sub-Licensing**: The Recipient shall not sublicense, sell, lease, or otherwise transfer Confidential Information to any third party without the Discloser’s written permission.  

8. **Compliance with Laws**: The Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws, regulations, and industry standards in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and privacy laws.  

9. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall promptly notify the Discloser in writing of any actual or suspected unauthorized disclosure, misuse, or loss of Confidential Information.  

10. **Return or Destruction**: Upon the Discloser’s request or termination of this Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all copies of Confidential Information and certify such destruction in writing.  

11. **No Competitive Use**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products, services, or strategies.  

12. **No Modification**: The Recipient shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works based on Confidential Information without the Discloser’s express written consent.  

13. **No Circumvention**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to circumvent the Discloser’s business relationships or opportunities.  

14. **No Employment Solicitation**: The Recipient shall not solicit or hire the Discloser’s employees or contractors based on Confidential Information.  

15. **Audit Rights**: The Discloser may, upon reasonable notice, audit the Recipient’s compliance with this Agreement, including inspections of records and facilities.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the effective date (the "Term"). Unless either party provides written notice of non-renewal at least thirty (30) days prior to the expiration of the Term, the Agreement shall automatically renew for successive one (1) year periods. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time, with or without cause, by providing thirty (30) days’ written notice to the other party.  

Notwithstanding termination or expiration, the Recipient’s obligations with respect to Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] from the date of disclosure, or longer if required by law. Upon termination, the Recipient shall cease all use of Confidential Information and, as directed by the Discloser, return or destroy such information. Sections pertaining to surviving obligations, remedies, and dispute resolution shall remain in force post-termination.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the Discloser shall be entitled to seek injunctive or other equitable relief to prevent or mitigate harm, without the necessity of posting a bond or proving actual damages. Such remedies shall be in addition to, and not in lieu of, any legal or monetary remedies available at law. The Discloser may also recover direct, consequential, and incidental damages resulting from the breach, including reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in enforcing this Agreement. The Recipient acknowledges that monetary damages may be inadequate to compensate for unauthorized disclosure and that injunctive relief is warranted to protect the Discloser’s interests.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising under or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its then-current rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 3
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or other form, that is either explicitly marked as confidential or, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to: (1) trade secrets, business strategies, and financial data; (2) product designs, technical specifications, and software code; (3) marketing plans, customer lists, and supplier relationships; (4) research and development projects; (5) any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known to the public.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all copies, extracts, summaries, or analyses of such information, regardless of who prepares them. Information is not considered Confidential if it: (a) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession before disclosure; (b) is or becomes publicly available without breach of this Agreement; (c) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully received from a third party without confidentiality obligations. The Receiving Party bears the burden of proving any exception applies.  

The parties acknowledge that unauthorized disclosure of Confidential Information could cause irreparable harm, including competitive injury, loss of goodwill, or financial damages. Accordingly, the Receiving Party agrees to exercise at least the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than reasonable care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as described in a separate written agreement or as mutually agreed in writing.  
2. **Internal Disclosure**: Confidential Information may be shared internally only with employees, contractors, or agents who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  
3. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, disassemble, or decompile any Confidential Information consisting of software or technical data.  
4. **No Copying**: Confidential Information shall not be copied, reproduced, or duplicated except as strictly necessary for the Authorized Purpose.  
5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Receiving Party shall not issue press releases, public statements, or marketing materials referencing the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information without prior written consent.  
6. **Data Security**: The Receiving Party shall implement industry-standard technical and organizational measures to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access, loss, or theft.  
7. **No Licensing**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any license, ownership, or rights to the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information beyond the Authorized Purpose.  
8. **Third-Party Restrictions**: The Receiving Party shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party, including subcontractors, without the Disclosing Party’s prior written approval.  
9. **Government Requests**: If legally compelled to disclose Confidential Information, the Receiving Party shall promptly notify the Disclosing Party to allow intervention, unless prohibited by law.  
10. **Return/Destruction**: Upon request or termination, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify compliance in writing.  
11. **No Competitive Use**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products, services, or strategies.  
12. **No Misrepresentation**: The Receiving Party shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information.  
13. **Audit Rights**: The Disclosing Party may audit the Receiving Party’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice.  
14. **No High-Risk Storage**: Confidential Information shall not be stored on personal devices or unsecured cloud platforms without encryption.  
15. **Survival of Obligations**: Restrictions on use and disclosure survive termination of this Agreement for as long as the information remains confidential.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [●] years from the Effective Date ("Initial Term"), unless earlier terminated as provided herein. Upon expiration of the Initial Term, the Agreement may be renewed for successive [●]-year terms by mutual written agreement. Either party may terminate this Agreement with [●] days’ prior written notice to the other party, provided such termination does not affect obligations with respect to Confidential Information disclosed prior to termination. The Disclosing Party may terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Receiving Party breaches any material term and fails to cure such breach within [●] days of notification. All obligations regarding Confidential Information shall survive termination for a period of [●] years, except for trade secrets, which shall remain protected indefinitely under applicable law. Termination shall not relieve the Receiving Party of its duty to return or destroy Confidential Information as required under this Agreement.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

The parties acknowledge that monetary damages may be insufficient to remedy a breach of this Agreement, and the Disclosing Party shall be entitled to seek injunctive or equitable relief, without posting a bond, to prevent actual or threatened breaches. In addition to such relief, the Disclosing Party may recover direct damages, including lost profits, and reasonable attorneys’ fees incurred in enforcing this Agreement. The Receiving Party shall indemnify the Disclosing Party for all losses arising from unauthorized disclosure, including third-party claims. Liability for breach shall not be limited except where prohibited by law. Any waiver of a breach shall not constitute a waiver of subsequent breaches. Remedies under this section are cumulative and not exclusive of any other rights available at law or in equity.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [●], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising under this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [●] under its commercial rules, with hearings held in [●]. The arbitrator’s award shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in the courts of [●], and the parties consent to the exclusive jurisdiction of such courts for such purposes. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable costs and attorneys’ fees. The United Nations Convention on Contracts for the International Sale of Goods shall not apply.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 4
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information ("Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, any data, materials, designs, specifications, business plans, financial information, trade secrets, technical know-how, software, processes, customer lists, marketing strategies, or any other information disclosed in any form (written, oral, electronic, or visual) that is marked as confidential or, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all information shared during the term of this Agreement, whether directly or indirectly, including information derived from or based on the original disclosure. Confidential Information also encompasses any notes, analyses, summaries, or other materials prepared by the Recipient that contain or reflect such information.  

Exclusions from Confidential Information include: (a) information already known to the Recipient at the time of disclosure, as evidenced by written records; (b) information that becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient; (c) information independently developed by the Recipient without reference to the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (d) information lawfully received from a third party without restriction on disclosure.  

The Recipient acknowledges that the Confidential Information is valuable and proprietary to the Discloser, and its unauthorized use or disclosure could cause irreparable harm. The Recipient agrees to exercise at least the same degree of care in safeguarding the Confidential Information as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but in no event less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: The Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or engaging in a business relationship with the Discloser, as mutually agreed in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information provided in object code or other proprietary formats.  

3. **No Copying**: The Recipient shall not copy, reproduce, or duplicate Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the permitted use and with prior written consent.  

4. **Limited Disclosure**: Confidential Information may only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or advisors who have a need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

5. **No Commercial Exploitation**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information for any commercial purpose outside the scope of this Agreement without express written permission.  

6. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement and maintain appropriate physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

7. **No Publicity**: The Recipient shall not issue any press releases, public announcements, or other communications referencing the Discloser or the Confidential Information without prior written consent.  

8. **Compliance with Laws**: The Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and export control laws.  

9. **No Transfer of Rights**: This Agreement does not grant the Recipient any rights, title, or interest in the Confidential Information, which remains the sole property of the Discloser.  

10. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

11. **No Circumvention**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to circumvent the Discloser’s business interests or gain a competitive advantage.  

12. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall immediately notify the Discloser in writing of any unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information and take all reasonable steps to mitigate harm.  

13. **No Subcontracting**: The Recipient shall not subcontract or delegate its obligations under this Agreement without the Discloser’s prior written approval.  

14. **No Modification**: The Recipient shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works based on Confidential Information without express written authorization.  

15. **Survival of Obligations**: The Recipient’s confidentiality obligations shall survive termination of this Agreement for the duration specified in Part 3.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [●] years from the effective date ("Initial Term"). Unless either party provides written notice of non-renewal at least [●] days prior to the expiration of the Initial Term, the Agreement shall automatically renew for successive [●]-year periods ("Renewal Term"). Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time, with or without cause, by providing [●] days’ written notice to the other party. Upon termination, the Recipient’s obligations under this Agreement shall continue with respect to Confidential Information disclosed during the term for a period of [●] years, unless otherwise agreed in writing.  

Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Discloser may terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Recipient breaches any material provision of this Agreement. Termination shall not relieve the Recipient of its obligations with respect to Confidential Information disclosed prior to termination. All provisions of this Agreement that, by their nature, should survive termination (including but not limited to confidentiality obligations, remedies for breach, and dispute resolution) shall remain in effect.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the Discloser shall be entitled to seek injunctive relief, including temporary restraining orders and preliminary or permanent injunctions, without the necessity of posting a bond or proving actual damages, in addition to any other remedies available at law or in equity. The Recipient acknowledges that monetary damages may be inadequate to compensate for the harm caused by unauthorized disclosure or use of Confidential Information and that injunctive relief is appropriate to prevent irreparable injury. The Discloser may also recover any direct damages, including lost profits, costs, and attorneys’ fees incurred as a result of the breach. The remedies set forth in this Agreement are cumulative and not exclusive of any other remedies available under applicable law.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [●], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising out of or relating to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [●] in accordance with its rules. The arbitration shall take place in [●], and the decision of the arbitrator(s) shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm. The prevailing party in any arbitration or legal proceeding shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [●] for any disputes not subject to arbitration.

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure and use of confidential information ("Confidential Information") exchanged between the parties. For the purposes of this Agreement, Confidential Information includes all non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means, that is designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential. This includes, but is not limited to, trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, product designs, technical specifications, software code, customer lists, marketing plans, and any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known or readily ascertainable by others.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all forms of communication, including documents, emails, presentations, demonstrations, and verbal discussions. It also covers any analyses, compilations, studies, or other materials prepared by the receiving party that contain or reflect Confidential Information. Information shall not be deemed confidential if it (a) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the receiving party; (b) was lawfully in the receiving party’s possession prior to disclosure; (c) is independently developed by the receiving party without reference to the disclosing party’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully obtained from a third party without restriction.  

The receiving party agrees to use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a potential business relationship with the disclosing party, as explicitly authorized in writing. The obligations under this Agreement shall survive any termination of discussions or agreements between the parties and shall remain in effect for the duration specified herein.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: Confidential Information may only be used for the specific business purpose disclosed in writing by the disclosing party, such as evaluating a potential partnership or collaboration.  

2. **Non-Disclosure**: The receiving party shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party without the prior written consent of the disclosing party, except as expressly permitted herein.  

3. **Internal Access**: Confidential Information may only be shared with employees, agents, or contractors of the receiving party who have a legitimate need to know and who are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as those herein.  

4. **No Reverse Engineering**: The receiving party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information provided in tangible or electronic form.  

5. **No Copying**: Confidential Information shall not be copied, reproduced, or duplicated except as necessary for the authorized purpose and with the disclosing party’s prior approval.  

6. **Security Measures**: The receiving party shall implement reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

7. **No Commercial Use**: Confidential Information shall not be used for any commercial purpose, including the development of competing products or services, without express written consent.  

8. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the receiving party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

9. **No Publicity**: The receiving party shall not issue any press releases, announcements, or other public statements referencing the disclosing party or the Confidential Information without prior written approval.  

10. **Compliance with Laws**: The receiving party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations, including data protection and export control laws, in handling Confidential Information.  

11. **No Modification**: Confidential Information shall not be altered, modified, or combined with other information without the disclosing party’s written consent.  

12. **No Subcontracting**: The receiving party shall not subcontract or delegate its obligations under this Agreement without the disclosing party’s prior written approval.  

13. **Notification of Breach**: The receiving party shall immediately notify the disclosing party upon discovering any unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information.  

14. **No Implied Licenses**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the receiving party any rights, titles, or licenses to the Confidential Information, except as expressly stated.  

15. **Survival of Obligations**: The restrictions and obligations herein shall survive termination of this Agreement for the duration specified in Part 3.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] from the effective date (the "Term"), unless earlier terminated as provided herein. The Term may be renewed by mutual written agreement of the parties for additional periods, subject to the same terms and conditions. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination becoming effective upon receipt of the notice. Upon termination, the receiving party’s obligations with respect to Confidential Information shall continue for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] from the date of termination, unless the Confidential Information no longer qualifies as such under the exclusions in Part 1. The disclosing party may also terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the receiving party breaches any material term hereof and fails to cure such breach within [insert cure period, e.g., thirty (30) days] of receiving written notice. All provisions of this Agreement that, by their nature, should survive termination (including but not limited to confidentiality obligations, remedies for breach, and dispute resolution) shall survive.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the disclosing party shall be entitled to seek injunctive or other equitable relief to prevent or restrain such breach, without the necessity of proving actual damages or posting a bond. Such remedies shall be in addition to, and not in lieu of, any legal or monetary remedies available at law or in equity. The disclosing party may also recover direct damages, including but not limited to lost profits, costs of mitigation, and reasonable attorneys’ fees incurred in enforcing this Agreement. The receiving party acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure of Confidential Information may cause irreparable harm for which monetary damages may be inadequate, and consents to the granting of injunctive relief. The parties agree that the remedies herein are cumulative and not exclusive, and the exercise of one remedy shall not preclude the exercise of others.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert governing law, e.g., the State of New York], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, state], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the state and federal courts located in [insert venue, e.g., New York County, New York] for any disputes not subject to arbitration. The prevailing party in any action to enforce this Agreement shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 6
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any data, materials, or knowledge disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party") that is not publicly available and is designated as confidential or would reasonably be considered confidential under the circumstances. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to: trade secrets, business strategies, financial records, product designs, technical specifications, software code, customer lists, marketing plans, and any other proprietary or sensitive information, whether conveyed verbally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all forms of communication, including memoranda, reports, emails, presentations, and any derivatives or analyses created by the Receiving Party based on such information. Information shall not be deemed confidential if it (a) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure, (b) is or becomes publicly available without breach of this Agreement, (c) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information, or (d) is rightfully obtained from a third party without confidentiality restrictions.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information could cause irreparable harm to the Disclosing Party. Accordingly, the Receiving Party agrees to exercise at least the same degree of care in safeguarding the Confidential Information as it employs for its own sensitive data, but no less than a reasonable standard of care. This obligation persists beyond the term of the Agreement for as long as the information remains confidential.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive underlying technology or methodologies.  
3. **Limited Access**: Access to Confidential Information shall be restricted to employees, contractors, or agents of the Receiving Party who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations.  
4. **No Copying**: The Receiving Party shall not reproduce Confidential Information in any form except as necessary for authorized use.  
5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Receiving Party shall not disclose Confidential Information to the public, media, or third parties without prior written consent.  
6. **Secure Storage**: Confidential Information must be stored securely, using encryption or physical safeguards, to prevent unauthorized access.  
7. **No Competitive Use**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products or services.  
8. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party must immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or breach.  
9. **Return or Destroy**: Upon request or termination of the Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify compliance.  
10. **No Sub-Licensing**: The Receiving Party shall not sublicense, assign, or transfer Confidential Information to any third party without express written permission.  
11. **Compliance with Laws**: All use of Confidential Information must comply with applicable laws, including data protection regulations.  
12. **No Misrepresentation**: The Receiving Party shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information.  
13. **No Unauthorized Modifications**: The Receiving Party shall not alter or modify Confidential Information without authorization.  
14. **No High-Risk Storage**: Confidential Information shall not be stored on unsecured cloud services or personal devices.  
15. **Audit Rights**: The Disclosing Party may audit the Receiving Party’s compliance with these restrictions upon reasonable notice.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [X] years from the Effective Date ("Term"), unless terminated earlier as provided herein. Either party may terminate the Agreement with [X] days’ written notice to the other party, provided such termination does not affect obligations accrued prior to termination. Upon expiration or termination, the Receiving Party’s duty to protect Confidential Information shall survive for [X] years or until the information becomes publicly available, whichever occurs first. The Agreement may be renewed by mutual written agreement, subject to updated terms. Termination does not relieve the Receiving Party of its obligations regarding previously disclosed Confidential Information. In the event of termination, the Disclosing Party may require the Receiving Party to certify in writing that all Confidential Information has been returned or destroyed. Failure to comply with these provisions constitutes a material breach of the Agreement.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the Disclosing Party shall be entitled to seek injunctive relief, without posting a bond, to prevent further unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information. Such remedies are in addition to, and not in lieu of, any monetary damages or other legal remedies available under law. The Receiving Party acknowledges that monetary damages alone may be insufficient to compensate for the harm caused by a breach, given the irreparable nature of such harm. The Disclosing Party may also recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in enforcing this Agreement. Liability for breach shall extend to direct and consequential damages, except where prohibited by law. The parties agree that any breach affecting trade secrets may also invoke penalties under applicable trade secret statutes.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [State/Country], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising under or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [Arbitration Institution] in [City, State/Country], under its then-current rules. The arbitration award shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in a court of law to prevent irreparable harm. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [Jurisdiction] for such purposes. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable legal fees and costs.

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, including but not limited to: (1) trade secrets, business strategies, marketing plans, financial data, and customer lists; (2) technical information such as software code, algorithms, patents, and product designs; (3) operational details, including manufacturing processes, supply chain logistics, and internal policies; (4) any other information marked or otherwise identified as confidential at the time of disclosure or which, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all derivatives, analyses, compilations, or summaries created by the Receiving Party that contain or reflect such information. However, Confidential Information excludes: (a) information already lawfully known to the Receiving Party prior to disclosure; (b) information independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; (c) information rightfully obtained from a third party without breach of confidentiality obligations; or (d) information that becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that the Confidential Information is valuable and constitutes a protectable business interest of the Disclosing Party. The Receiving Party agrees to use the Confidential Information solely for the purpose of [describe permitted purpose, e.g., evaluating a potential business relationship] and not for any competitive or unauthorized purpose. Unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information may cause irreparable harm to the Disclosing Party, entitling them to equitable relief in addition to legal remedies.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Receiving Party may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of [specific permitted use], as agreed in writing by the Disclosing Party. Any deviation requires prior written consent.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components or methodologies.  
3. **Limited Access**: Confidential Information shall only be accessible to employees, contractors, or agents of the Receiving Party who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as stringent as this Agreement.  
4. **No Copying**: The Receiving Party shall not reproduce, duplicate, or copy Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the authorized purpose, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  
5. **No Unauthorized Disclosure**: The Receiving Party shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party without the Disclosing Party’s prior written approval.  
6. **Security Measures**: The Receiving Party shall implement reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  
7. **No Publicity**: The Receiving Party shall not issue press releases, marketing materials, or other public statements referencing the Confidential Information or the parties’ relationship without written consent.  
8. **Return or Destruction**: Upon termination of the Agreement or the Disclosing Party’s request, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  
9. **No License Granted**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any rights, title, or license to the Confidential Information, including intellectual property rights.  
10. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and export control laws.  
11. **No Circumvention**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to circumvent the Disclosing Party’s business interests or gain a competitive advantage.  
12. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party shall immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information.  
13. **No Transfer**: The Receiving Party shall not assign, transfer, or sublicense its rights or obligations under this Agreement without the Disclosing Party’s written consent.  
14. **Audit Rights**: The Disclosing Party may audit the Receiving Party’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice and during normal business hours.  
15. **Survival of Obligations**: The Receiving Party’s confidentiality obligations shall survive termination of this Agreement for any reason.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"). Unless either party provides written notice of non-renewal at least [insert notice period, e.g., thirty (30) days] prior to the expiration of the Term, the Agreement shall automatically renew for successive [insert renewal period, e.g., one (1) year] terms. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time, with or without cause, by providing [insert notice period, e.g., thirty (30) days] written notice to the other party. Upon termination, the Receiving Party’s obligations with respect to Confidential Information shall continue indefinitely for trade secrets and for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] for all other Confidential Information.  

Termination of this Agreement shall not relieve the Receiving Party of its obligations to protect Confidential Information disclosed during the Term. The Disclosing Party may terminate the Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Receiving Party breaches any material term of this Agreement and fails to cure such breach within [insert cure period, e.g., fifteen (15) days] of receiving written notice. Sections addressing confidentiality obligations, remedies, and dispute resolution shall survive termination.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the Disclosing Party shall be entitled to seek injunctive or other equitable relief to prevent or mitigate harm, without the necessity of posting a bond or proving actual damages. Such remedies shall be in addition to, and not in lieu of, any legal or monetary remedies available at law. The Disclosing Party may recover direct damages, including lost profits and costs incurred due to the breach, as well as reasonable attorneys’ fees and litigation expenses. The Receiving Party acknowledges that monetary damages may be insufficient to remedy a breach and agrees that injunctive relief is appropriate.  

If the Receiving Party fails to comply with its obligations under this Agreement, the Disclosing Party may also require the Receiving Party to disgorge any profits derived from the unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information. The parties agree that the harm caused by a breach may be irreparable and that the Disclosing Party shall not be required to post a bond to obtain injunctive relief. The remedies herein are cumulative and not exclusive of any other rights or remedies available under law or equity.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert governing law jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively in the [insert court venue, e.g., state or federal courts located in Los Angeles County, California], and the parties irrevocably submit to the jurisdiction of such courts.  

Alternatively, if arbitration is preferred: "Any dispute arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration provider, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert location, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction." The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. The parties waive any right to a jury trial in any proceeding arising out of this Agreement.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 8
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, any non-public, sensitive, or proprietary information disclosed in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, whether or not marked as confidential.  

For purposes of this Agreement, Confidential Information encompasses:  
1. **Business Strategies**: Plans, forecasts, marketing strategies, and financial data.  
2. **Technical Data**: Software code, algorithms, patents, trade secrets, and research.  
3. **Product Information**: Designs, prototypes, specifications, and development processes.  
4. **Customer and Supplier Data**: Lists, contracts, pricing, and relationships.  
5. **Operational Details**: Processes, methodologies, and internal policies.  
6. **Intellectual Property**: Copyrights, trademarks, and unpublished creative works.  

Confidential Information excludes:  
1. Information already publicly available or lawfully obtained from a third party without restriction.  
2. Information independently developed by the Recipient without reference to the Discloser’s Confidential Information.  
3. Information disclosed with the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

The Recipient acknowledges that Confidential Information is valuable and constitutes a competitive advantage for the Discloser. The scope of this Agreement extends to all disclosures made during the term, including pre-existing information shared under this Agreement. The Recipient agrees to treat Confidential Information with at least the same degree of care as its own sensitive information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **Internal Disclosure**: Confidential Information may be shared only with employees, contractors, or agents who need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations.  
3. **No Reverse Engineering**: Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components.  
4. **No Copying**: Recipient shall not copy, reproduce, or duplicate Confidential Information except as necessary for the authorized purpose.  
5. **No Public Disclosure**: Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to the public, media, or third parties without prior written consent.  
6. **Security Measures**: Recipient shall implement reasonable physical, electronic, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information.  
7. **No Unauthorized Modifications**: Recipient shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works from Confidential Information without permission.  
8. **Notification of Breach**: Recipient must promptly notify Discloser of any unauthorized access, use, or disclosure of Confidential Information.  
9. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination, Recipient shall return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify compliance.  
10. **No Competitive Use**: Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to gain a competitive advantage or harm Discloser’s business.  
11. **No Solicitation**: Recipient shall not solicit Discloser’s employees, customers, or partners using Confidential Information.  
12. **Compliance with Laws**: Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information.  
13. **No Sub-Licensing**: Recipient shall not sublicense, assign, or transfer Confidential Information without Discloser’s written consent.  
14. **Limited Duration**: Restrictions apply for the duration of the Agreement and any post-termination survival period.  
15. **No Implied Rights**: No license or ownership rights are granted under this Agreement.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [●] years from the Effective Date ("Initial Term"). Upon expiration of the Initial Term, the Agreement may be renewed for successive [●]-year terms by mutual written agreement of both parties. Either party may terminate this Agreement with [●] days’ written notice to the other party, provided such termination does not affect obligations accrued prior to termination.  

Notwithstanding termination, the Recipient’s duty to protect Confidential Information shall survive for [●] years after termination or until the Confidential Information becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient, whichever occurs first. The Discloser may terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Recipient breaches any material term, subject to cure periods where applicable. Upon termination, the Recipient shall cease all use of Confidential Information and comply with return or destruction requirements.  

#part 4  
**Remedies for Breach**  

In the event of a breach or threatened breach of this Agreement, the Discloser shall be entitled to seek injunctive relief, including temporary restraining orders and preliminary or permanent injunctions, without the necessity of posting a bond or proving actual damages. Such remedies shall be in addition to, and not in lieu of, any monetary damages or other legal remedies available at law or in equity. The Discloser may also recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in enforcing this Agreement.  

The Recipient acknowledges that monetary damages may be inadequate to compensate for unauthorized disclosure of Confidential Information due to its unique and irreplaceable nature. Accordingly, the Discloser’s right to equitable relief shall not be prejudiced by its pursuit of other remedies. The parties agree that any breach of this Agreement may cause irreparable harm, warranting immediate judicial intervention.  

#part 5  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [●], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising under or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [●] under its commercial arbitration rules, with hearings held in [●]. The arbitral award shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction.  

Alternatively, if arbitration is not enforced, the parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the state and federal courts located in [●] for any legal action. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. The parties waive any right to a jury trial and agree to resolve disputes on an individual basis, not as part of a class action.

##prompt_id: 2, type: segmented, sample_id: 1
********
#part 1  
**Chapter 1: The Unseen Burden**  
Elena Vasquez, a 32-year-old investigative journalist, returns to her hometown of Silver Creek after a decade away. The town, once vibrant, now feels suffocating under the weight of secrets. Her father, a retired police officer, died under mysterious circumstances, and the official report—a heart attack—doesn’t sit right with her. Elena’s sharp instincts tell her there’s more to the story. As she sorts through his belongings, she finds a cryptic note hidden in his old desk: *"The mayor knows the truth."* The conflict is set: Elena must uncover what really happened to her father, even if it means confronting the powerful figures who run Silver Creek. Her journey begins with a single question: Who can she trust?  

#part 2  
**Chapter 2: Tangled Webs**  
Elena reconnects with her childhood friend, Daniel, now a local reporter. He warns her about digging too deep—the mayor, Richard Holloway, has ties to shady business deals and a reputation for silencing dissent. Meanwhile, Elena meets an elderly neighbor, Mrs. Peña, who hints at her father’s involvement in a cold case from 20 years ago. As Elena pieces together fragments of the past, she attracts unwanted attention. Her apartment is ransacked, and a shadowy figure follows her. Daniel, initially reluctant, agrees to help after realizing the danger she’s in. Their friendship deepens into a tentative alliance, but Elena senses he’s hiding something. The rising action builds as Elena discovers a hidden file in her father’s storage unit—a list of names, all connected to a long-buried scandal.  

#part 3  
**Chapter 3: The Betrayal**  
Elena confronts Daniel about the file, accusing him of knowing more than he’s letting on. He confesses: her father was investigating corruption in the police force, and Daniel’s own father, a retired detective, was implicated. Before they can act, Elena receives a call from Mrs. Peña, who claims to have proof of the mayor’s involvement in her father’s death. But when Elena arrives, she finds Mrs. Peña’s house in flames—and the old woman inside. The tragedy shakes Elena to her core. The reversal is stark: her ally is compromised, her only lead is dead, and the mayor’s enforcers are closing in. Elena realizes she’s running out of time—and options.  

#part 4  
**Chapter 4: Truth and Consequences**  
Elena goes rogue, leaking the file to the press and broadcasting a damning exposé live on social media. The town erupts in chaos as the mayor’s empire crumbles. Cornered, Holloway confronts Elena in a tense standoff at the abandoned steel mill—the same place her father was last seen alive. He admits to ordering her father’s murder to cover up embezzlement and a decades-old murder. Just as Holloway pulls a gun, Daniel arrives with the police, having finally chosen justice over loyalty. Holloway is arrested, and Elena’s father’s name is cleared. In the aftermath, Elena decides to stay in Silver Creek, rebuilding her life and honoring her father’s legacy by starting an independent news outlet. The resolution is bittersweet: justice is served, but the cost was high. Elena finds closure—and a new purpose.

##prompt_id: 2, type: segmented, sample_id: 2
********
#part 1  
**Chapter 1: The Unseen Burden**  
Elena Vasquez, a 32-year-old investigative journalist, returns to her hometown of Crestwood after a decade away. The town, once vibrant, now feels hollow—its streets lined with boarded-up shops and wary faces. Elena is here to uncover the truth behind her father’s sudden death, ruled a suicide but shrouded in inconsistencies. As she sifts through his old notes, she finds a cryptic message: "The river knows." Her father, a retired environmental scientist, had been studying the local river’s contamination before his death. Elena’s conflict is twofold: confronting her grief and the growing suspicion that his death was no accident. When she visits the riverbank at dusk, she spots a shadowy figure watching her—a silent confirmation that someone doesn’t want her digging deeper.  

#part 2  
**Chapter 2: Tangled Currents**  
Elena reconnects with Daniel Reyes, her childhood friend and now a local mechanic. He warns her to drop the investigation, hinting at dangerous forces at play. Their bond rekindles, but trust is fragile—Daniel’s brother works for the powerful Mercer Corporation, the prime suspect in the river’s pollution. Meanwhile, Elena interviews townspeople, uncovering a pattern of silenced dissent. A retired nurse, Mrs. O’Donnell, confides that Elena’s father had been receiving anonymous threats. One night, Elena’s apartment is ransacked, her father’s research stolen. Daniel arrives unexpectedly, offering shelter. As they piece together clues, they realize the contamination is worse than reported, and the cover-up goes beyond Crestwood. The tension escalates when Daniel’s brother confronts them, torn between loyalty and conscience.  

#part 3  
**Chapter 3: The Breaking Point**  
Elena and Daniel sneak into Mercer’s restricted facility, finding documents proving illegal waste dumping—and a list of names, including her father’s. As they flee, security spots them. A chase ensues, ending with Daniel gravely injured. Elena barely escapes, but the evidence is lost. Devastated, she questions whether the truth is worth the cost. At the hospital, Daniel urges her to run, but Elena refuses. She receives a call from an anonymous tipster offering a final piece of the puzzle: a hidden water sample her father left behind. The reversal is clear—Elena must choose between safety and justice. She retrieves the sample, but Mercer’s enforcers close in. Cornered, she transmits the data to a trusted colleague just as the screen goes black.  

#part 4  
**Chapter 4: The River’s Truth**  
The leaked data sparks public outrage. National media descend on Crestwood, forcing authorities to act. Mercer’s CEO is arrested, and the EPA launches a cleanup. Elena, though bruised, is hailed as a hero—but her victory is bittersweet. Daniel survives, but their friendship is strained by the risks taken. At her father’s grave, Elena finally grieves, realizing his legacy wasn’t just the truth but her courage to seek it. She publishes an exposé, honoring his work. In the final scene, she stands by the river, now slated for restoration, and tosses in a single flower—a promise to keep fighting for the unseen. The town begins to heal, and so does she.

##prompt_id: 2, type: segmented, sample_id: 3
********
#part 1  
**Chapter 1: The Unseen Burden**  
Elena Vasquez, a 28-year-old investigative journalist, returns to her hometown of Crestwood after a decade away. Haunted by the unsolved disappearance of her younger sister, Sofia, she carries guilt for leaving her family behind to pursue her career. Crestwood, a sleepy coastal town, greets her with wary eyes—locals whisper about the "Crestwood Curse," a series of unexplained vanishings over the years. Elena’s father, a retired detective, refuses to discuss Sofia’s case, deepening the rift between them. When Elena discovers a cryptic note hidden in her childhood home—a faded drawing of a lighthouse with the words "Find me"—she becomes obsessed with uncovering the truth. The chapter ends with Elena standing at the edge of the town’s abandoned lighthouse, the wind howling as she vows to confront the past.  

#part 2  
**Chapter 2: Tangled Threads**  
Elena reconnects with Daniel Reyes, her childhood friend and now a local police officer, who reluctantly agrees to help her investigate. Their strained relationship is complicated by unspoken feelings and Daniel’s fear of reopening old wounds. As Elena digs deeper, she uncovers a pattern: every disappearance coincides with the town’s annual festival, "The Tide’s Call." She interviews Marisol, an elderly woman who claims to have seen Sofia the night she vanished, but Marisol’s cryptic warnings about "the watchers in the waves" leave Elena unsettled. Meanwhile, Elena’s father warns her to stop, hinting at dangers she doesn’t understand. Tension builds when Elena receives an anonymous message: a photo of Sofia’s bracelet, recently taken, with the lighthouse in the background. The chapter ends with Elena and Daniel breaking into the restricted lighthouse at midnight.  

#part 3  
**Chapter 3: The Truth in the Tide**  
Inside the lighthouse, Elena and Daniel find a hidden basement filled with disturbing artifacts—old newspapers, personal belongings of the missing, and a map marking locations along the coast. A sudden noise startles them; someone else is here. They’re ambushed by a shadowy figure, and Daniel is knocked unconscious. Elena flees, but not before recognizing the attacker: Mayor Grayson, a family friend. Betrayed and terrified, she realizes the town’s leadership is involved. Elena escapes to Marisol’s home, where the old woman reveals the horrifying truth—the disappearances are sacrifices to appease something lurking in the ocean, a tradition upheld for generations. The chapter ends with Elena staring at the churning waves, realizing Sofia might still be alive—but not human.  

#part 4  
**Chapter 4: The Last Sacrifice**  
Elena confronts Mayor Grayson during the festival, exposing his crimes to the townspeople. Chaos erupts as the crowd turns on him, but the ritual has already begun—the ocean surges, and eerie figures emerge from the water. Elena spots Sofia among them, her eyes glowing with an otherworldly light. Daniel arrives, injured but determined, and together they disrupt the ritual using artifacts from the lighthouse. The creatures retreat, but Sofia lingers, placing a locket in Elena’s hand before vanishing into the mist. In the aftermath, Crestwood is forever changed—Grayson is arrested, and the town grapples with its dark legacy. Elena publishes her findings, honoring Sofia’s memory and freeing herself from guilt. The novel ends with Elena and Daniel watching the sunrise over the ocean, a new beginning on the horizon.

##prompt_id: 2, type: segmented, sample_id: 4
********
#part 1  
**Chapter 1: The Broken Compass**  
Elias Carter, a disgraced cartographer with a haunted past, arrives in the remote coastal town of Blackthorn Cove. Once celebrated for his precision, Elias now drowns in self-doubt after a fatal error in his maps led to a doomed expedition. The townsfolk whisper about the "Cursed Cartographer," but he ignores them, focused on his last chance: charting the uncharted Veil Isles, a treacherous cluster of islands shrouded in legend. When Elias discovers an ancient map fragment in the town’s derelict archives—one that contradicts all known records—he realizes the islands might hold more than just rocks and tides. But the fragment is incomplete, and the town’s reclusive lighthouse keeper, Mara, warns him that some secrets are best left buried. Elias ignores her, setting sail at dawn. The conflict is set: will his obsession redeem or destroy him?  

#part 2  
**Chapter 2: The Lighthouse Keeper’s Secret**  
As Elias navigates the Veil Isles’ fog-bound waters, his boat is dashed against the rocks. He awakens in Mara’s lighthouse, where she grudgingly tends to his wounds. Mara, a former sailor with a sharp tongue and sharper instincts, reveals she once sought the islands’ secrets too—until her crew vanished. A tentative alliance forms: she’ll help Elias decode the map if he promises to turn back if they uncover "the wrong kind of truth." Meanwhile, Elias’s nightmares intensify, filled with whispers of a drowned crew and a glowing rift beneath the waves. When they decipher the map’s clues—a tidal cave marked with a symbol matching Elias’s family crest—Mara panics. The crest, she claims, is tied to the old legends of the "Tidecaller," a being said to control the sea itself. Elias scoffs, but as they enter the cave at low tide, the water behind them begins to rise unnaturally fast.  

#part 3  
**Chapter 3: The Turning Tide**  
Trapped in the cave, Elias and Mara barely escape the rushing water, but not before Elias glimpses something impossible: a humanoid figure woven from swirling currents, watching them from the depths. Mara confesses the truth—the Tidecaller is real, and Elias’s ancestor bound it to their bloodline to control the seas. The failed expedition? A consequence of Elias unknowingly breaking the pact by mischarting sacred waters. The creature is now free, and it’s hunting him. Elias’s guilt hardens into resolve; he refuses to let more die for his mistakes. As storms batter the coast, he finds Mara preparing to flee. "You don’t understand," she snaps. "It doesn’t want revenge. It wants you to replace it." The revelation staggers Elias: to save the town, he must become the thing he fears.  

#part 4  
**Chapter 4: The Last Chart**  
In the climax, Elias returns to the cave at high tide, alone. The Tidecaller emerges, offering power in exchange for his humanity. Meanwhile, Mara rallies the townsfolk to evacuate as the sea devours the shore. Just as Elias begins to succumb, he remembers Mara’s words: "Some bonds aren’t chains." Instead of accepting the creature’s deal, he severs the bloodline’s tie by burning the ancient map—and his own charts—in a ritual of surrender. The Tidecaller shrieks as the pact dissolves, the waves stilling instantly. Days later, Elias wakes on the beach, the sea calm and the creature gone. Blackthorn Cove is saved, but his hands are now marked with faint, swirling scars. Mara finds him staring at the horizon. "What now?" she asks. Elias smiles ruefully. "I chart the things that can’t be mapped." The resolution: Elias embraces uncertainty, Mara stays as his first mate, and the sea keeps its secrets—for now.

The resolution is bittersweet—justice is served, but the cost lingers. Despite their clashing personalities—Lena’s stubborn hope versus Daniel’s rigid logic—they form an uneasy alliance. The journal leads them to interview elderly locals, who share fragmented stories of drownings and eerie lights over the water. One night, Lena dreams of Eli calling her from the cave mentioned in the journal. She wakes to find her hands covered in saltwater and sand, though her door was locked. Daniel dismisses it as stress, but Lena becomes convinced supernatural forces are at play. Before she can process it, the cave begins flooding rapidly. Daniel pulls her to safety, but not before she sees Eli’s face in the swirling water—alive, but changed. In the chaos, Eli reappears, no longer human but at peace. He helps Lena and Daniel escape as the cave collapses. With the curse broken, Havenbrook’s storms cease. Lena publishes Eli’s journal, exposing the town’s secrets. Though she mourns, she finds solace in honoring his memory. Daniel stays, and together they reopen her bookstore, now a beacon for stories—both light and dark. The tide, once a threat, becomes a symbol of renewal.

##prompt_id: 3, type: segmented, sample_id: 3
